namePattern = /([A-Z]+,\\s*[A-Z])\\s+.*?\\1/;\n    const match = allText.match(namePattern);\n    \n    if (match) {\n      // Find the second occurrence and replace with SOLO\n      const divs =         console.log(\'DFP-NEO: Fixed solo flight for\', match[1]);\n          } else {\n            foundFirst = true;\n          }\n        }\n      });\n    }\n  });\n}\n\n// Grey course fix -
